  <span m='410480'>basically</span> <span m='410870'>assigns</span> <span m='411140'>gradients</span>
  <span m='411675'>to</span> <span m='411940'>groups of</span> <span m='412310'>pixels</span>

  <span m='637370'>basically</span> <span m='637770'>a sum</span> <span m='638130'>of

  <span m='639260'>gratings</span> <span m='640580'>that</span> <span m='640820'>differ,</span>

  <span m='864730'>inside</span> <span m='865120'>of</span> <span m='865240'>a</span>
  <span m='865300'>cell,</span> <span m='865720'>or</span> <span m='865870'>a</span>
  <span m='865960'>neuron.</span> <span m='867640'>The</span> <span m='868030'>sum</span>
  <span m='868470'>here</span> <span m='868720'>is</span> <span m='868860'>not</span>
  <span m='869070'>just a</span> <span m='869450'>regular</span> <span m='869890'>sum,</span>
  <span m='870220'>it's</span> <span m='870360'>a</span> <span m='870550'>weighted</span>
  <span m='870880'>sum.</span> <span m='871190'>So</span> <span m='871420'>the</span>
  <span m='871570'>neuron</span> <span m='872000'>specifies</span> <span m='872680'>some</span>
  <span m='873070'>weight,</span> <span m='873950'>which</span> <span m='874210'>you</span>
  <span m='874330'>can</span> <span m='874480'>think</span> <span m='874720'>of</span>
  <span m='874900'>as</span> <span m='875260'>how</span> <span m='875440'>much</span>
  <span m='875650'>it</span> <span m='875770'>values</span> <span m='876460'>the</span>
  <span m='876640'>input</span> <span m='877090'>coming</span> <span m='877540'>from</span>
  <span m='877850'>a</span> <span m='877960'>specific</span> <span m='879390'>neuron,</span>
  <span m='879940'>and</span> <span m='880060'>then</span> <span m='880540'>the</span>
  <span m='880720'>input is</span> <span m='881160'>multiplied</span> <span m='881740'>by</span>
  <span m='881980'>its</span> <span m='882190'>weight,</span> <span m='882700'>and</span>
  <span m='882790'>then</span> <span m='883360'>the</span> <span m='883480'>total</span>
  <span m='883840'>sum</span> <span m='884230'>that</span> <span m='884800'>the neuron</span>
  <span m='885070'>computes</span> <span m='885640'>is</span> <span m='885760'>then</span>
  <span m='886000'>fed</span> <span m='886360'>into</span> <span m='886720'>an</span>
  <span m='886870'>activation</span> <span m='887560'>function</span> <span m='888430'>that</span>
  <span m='888820'>produces</span> <span m='889360'>the</span> <span m='889540'>output</span>
  <span m='890310'>that</span> <span m='890550'>the</span> <span m='890830'>neuron</span>
  <span m='891870'>then</span> <span m='892150'>basically</span> <span m='892650'>produces.</span>
  </p><p><span m='895690'>Now,</span> <span m='896020'>what</span> <span m='896200'>we</span>
  <span m='896320'>just</span> <span m='896530'>saw</span> <span m='896780'>here</span>
  <span m='897170'>is</span> <span m='897590'>really</span> <span m='897920'>a</span>
  <span m='898010'>simple</span> <span m='898550'>neuron,</span> <span m='898740'>a</span>
  <span m='898870'>single</span> <span m='899230'>neuron.</span> <span m='899950'>You</span>
  <span m='900070'>can't</span> <span m='900290'>really</span> <span m='900520'>do</span>
  <span m='900700'>much</span> <span m='901090'>with</span> <span m='901300'>just</span>
  <span m='901600'>one</span> <span m='901870'>neuron,</span> <span m='902570'>so</span>
  <span m='902630'>what</span> <span m='902870'>you would</span> <span m='903070'>do</span>
  <span m='903310'>is</span> <span m='903670'>combined</span> <span m='904210'>these</span>
  <span m='904430'>neurons</span> <span m='904710'>in</span> <span m='904880'>a</span>
  <span m='905190'>certain</span> <span m='905560'>topography,</span> <span m='906390'>or</span>
  <span m='907030'>in</span> <span m='907120'>that</span> <span m='907360'>case,</span>
  <span m='907750'>we</span> <span m='907900'>have</span> <span m='908370'>a</span>
  <span m='908560'>network</span> <span m='910010'>with</span> <span m='910390'>seven</span>
  <span m='910660'>neurons</span> <span m='911650'>organized</span> <span m='912130'>in</span>
  <span m='912250'>three</span> <span m='912460'>different</span> <span m='912790'>layers.</span>
  <span m='913730'>And</span> <span m='914020'>what you</span> <span m='914200'>can</span>
  <span m='914650'>think</span> <span m='915490'>of</span> <span m='915670'>that</span>
  <span m='915970'>is really</span> <span m='916430'>as</span> <span m='916790'>one</span>
  <span m='917000'>big</span> <span m='917270'>neuron</span> <span m='917960'>with</span>
  <span m='918260'>12</span> <span m='918620'>inputs,</span> <span m='919310'>and</span>
  <span m='919430'>one</span> <span m='919730'>output.</span> </p><p><span m='920790'>So</span>
  <span m='921140'>for</span> <span m='921260'>example,</span> <span m='921840'>in</span>
  <span m='921940'>the</span> <span m='921950'>case</span> <span m='922190'>of</span>
  <span m='922310'>the</span> <span m='922430'>chair</span> <span m='922910'>that</span>
  <span m='923060'>was</span> <span m='923240'>previously</span> <span m='923600'>mentioned,</span>
  <span m='924030'>if</span> <span m='924140'>you're</span> <span m='924380'>trying</span>
  <span m='924740'>to</span> <span m='924920'>identify</span> <span m='926150'>whether</span>
  <span m='926510'>a</span> <span m='926540'>specific</span> <span m='927260'>image</span>
  <span m='927620'>has</span> <span m='927890'>a</span> <span m='927950'>chair</span>
  <span m='928430'>in</span> <span m='928550'>it</span> <span m='928760'>or</span>
  <span m='928910'>not,</span> <span m='930200'>these</span> <span m='930590'>12</span>
  <span m='931010'>inputs</span> <span m='931400'>here</span> <span m='931670'>could</span>
  <span m='931850'>be</span> <span m='932120'>some</span> <span m='932390'>sub</span>
  <span m='932780'>images,</span> <span m='933380'>or</span> <span m='933560'>some</span>
  <span m='933950'>small</span> <span m='934670'>areas</span> <span m='935060'>of</span>
  <span m='935150'>the</span> <span m='935270'>initial</span> <span m='935630'>image</span>
  <span m='936260'>that</span> <span m='936380'>you</span> <span m='936530'>feed</span>
  <span m='936860'>into</span> <span m='937100'>the</span> <span m='937190'>network,</span>
  <span m='938030'>and</span> <span m='938600'>the</span> <span m='938810'>output</span>
  <span m='939170'>here</span> <span m='939500'>could</span> <span m='939700'>be a</span>
  <span m='940070'>yes</span> <span m='940550'>or</span> <span m='940760'>no.</span>
  <span m='941100'>Whether</span> <span m='941360'>the</span> <span m='941660'>image</span>
  <span m='941990'>has</span> <span m='942230'>a</span> <span m='942290'>chair,</span>

  <span m='943310'>a</span> <span m='943340'>chair.</span> <span m='944480'>And</span>
  <span m='944600'>that</span> <span m='944730'>is</span> <span m='944940'>really</span>
  <span m='945240'>the</span> <span m='945350'>concept</span> <span m='945830'>behind</span>
  <span m='946330'>convolutional</span> <span m='946950'>neural</span> <span m='947250'>networks,</span>
  <span m='947750'>which</span> <span m='947990'>we'll</span> <span m='948200'>go</span>
  <span m='948410'>into</span> <span m='949300'>details</span> <span m='949700'>in
  a bit.</span> </p><p><span m='952040'>So</span> <span m='953030'>what</span> <span

  <span m='954080'>doing</span> <span m='954540'>in</span> <span m='954680'>that</span>
  <span m='954920'>case,</span> <span m='955460'>is</span> <span m='955670'>really</span>
  <span m='956000'>just</span> <span m='956240'>performing</span> <span m='956610'>a</span>
  <span m='956980'>dot</span> <span m='957270'>product,</span> <span m='958600'>which</span>

  <span m='962330'>each</span> <span m='962540'>of</span> <span m='962630'>the</span>
  <span m='962750'>other</span> <span m='962930'>neurons,</span> <span m='964140'>you</span>
  <span m='964350'>would</span> <span m='964480'>obtain</span> <span m='964760'>a</span>
  <span m='964970'>convolution.</span> <span m='965960'>So</span> <span m='966140'>what</span>
  <span m='966260'>we</span> <span m='966410'>have</span> <span m='966710'>here</span>

  <span m='968420'>If</span> <span m='968630'>the</span> <span m='968780'>input,</span>
  <span m='969070'>in</span> <span m='969200'>that</span> <span m='969440'>case,</span>
  <span m='970010'>is</span> <span m='970160'>an</span> <span m='970280'>image</span>
  <span m='970700'>or</span> <span m='970860'>a</span> <span m='970910'>sub</span>
  <span m='971210'>image,</span> <span m='971810'>then</span> <span m='971930'>the</span>

  <span m='978080'>is</span> <span m='978230'>the</span> <span m='978380'>filter</span>

  <span m='979520'>in</span> <span m='979610'>the</span> <span m='979730'>convolution.</span>
  </p><p><span m='980930'>And</span> <span m='981050'>then</span> <span m='981450'>the</span>
  <span m='981580'>sum</span> <span m='981940'>here</span> <span m='982220'>would</span>
  <span m='982340'>be</span> <span m='982550'>the</span> <span m='982670'>dot</span>
  <span m='982940'>product</span> <span m='983480'>of</span> <span m='983600'>the</span>
  <span m='983720'>weights</span> <span m='984100'>and the</span> <span m='984513'>inputs,</span>
  <span m='985340'>and</span> <span m='985460'>that</span> <span m='985720'>sum</span>
  <span m='986060'>would</span> <span m='986180'>be</span> <span m='986330'>computed</span>
  <span m='986810'>by</span> <span m='986990'>a</span> <span m='987020'>specific</span>
  <span m='987650'>neuron</span> <span m='988040'>in</span> <span m='988130'>your</span>
  <span m='988280'>network.</span> <span m='990110'>Then,</span> <span m='990820'>that</span>

  <span m='991340'>convolution</span> <span m='992000'>step,</span> <span m='993710'>and</span>
  <span m='993860'>then</span> <span m='994070'>that</span> <span m='994310'>convolution</span>
  <span m='994940'>step</span> <span m='995780'>would</span> <span m='995990'>happen</span>
  <span m='996440'>at</span> <span m='996650'>the</span> <span m='996740'>first</span>
  <span m='997130'>layer</span> <span m='997570'>in</span> <span m='997670'>the network.</span>
  <span m='998010'>So you</span> <span m='998220'>would be</span> <span m='998390'>applying</span>
  <span m='998810'>this</span> <span m='998990'>to</span> <span m='999110'>the</span>
  <span m='999250'>input,</span> <span m='999470'>but</span> <span m='999750'>you</span>
  <span m='999890'>also</span> <span m='1000310'>would be</span> <span m='1000550'>applying</span>
  <span m='1000835'>this</span> <span m='1001120'>at the</span> <span m='1001210'>second</span>
  <span m='1001630'>layer,</span> <span m='1001840'>and</span> <span m='1002020'>third</span>
  <span m='1002300'>layer.</span> <span m='1002770'>In that</span> <span m='1003180'>case,</span>
  <span m='1003370'>we're only</span> <span m='1003640'>showing</span> <span m='1004030'>what</span>
  <span m='1004240'>happens</span> <span m='1004710'>in</span> <span m='1004810'>the</span>
  <span m='1004900'>first</span> <span m='1005260'>layer.</span> </p><p><span m='1007030'>The</span>
  <span m='1007150'>next</span> <span m='1007520'>step</span> <span m='1007780'>after</span>
  <span m='1008110'>the</span> <span m='1008230'>convolution</span> <span m='1008590'>would</span>
  <span m='1008950'>be</span> <span m='1009160'>the</span> <span m='1009490'>activation</span>
  <span m='1010150'>step.</span> <span m='1010720'>So</span> <span m='1011490'>the</span>
  <span m='1011700'>dot</span> <span m='1012055'>product</span> <span m='1012410'>computed</span>
  <span m='1012990'>here</span> <span m='1013980'>would</span> <span m='1014470'>be</span>
  <span m='1014940'>there's</span> <span m='1015150'>a</span> <span m='1015220'>function</span>
  <span m='1015660'>that</span> <span m='1015760'>would</span> <span m='1015860'>be</span>
  <span m='1015880'>applied</span> <span m='1016490'>to</span> <span m='1016690'>the</span>
  <span m='1016810'>sum,</span> <span m='1017470'>and</span> <span m='1017560'>then</span>
  <span m='1018430'>that</span> <span m='1018640'>function</span> <span m='1018940'>would</span>
  <span m='1019030'>produce</span> <span m='1019420'>the</span> <span m='1019600'>output</span>
  <span m='1020180'>of</span> <span m='1020350'>the</span> <span m='1020470'>neuron.</span>
  <span m='1022730'>And</span> <span m='1022810'>this</span> <span m='1022990'>is</span>
  <span m='1023110'>where</span> <span m='1023290'>the</span> <span m='1023440'>activation</span>
  <span m='1024310'>layer</span> <span m='1024760'>is.</span> <span m='1025030'>You</span>
  <span m='1025130'>also</span> <span m='1025339'>have</span> <span m='1025480'>another</span>
  <span m='1025800'>activation</span> <span m='1026380'>layer</span> <span m='1026710'>here,</span>

  <span m='1032319'>What</span> <span m='1032560'>we</span> <span m='1032680'>just</span>
  <span m='1032920'>went</span> <span m='1033160'>through</span> <span m='1033470'>now</span>

  <span m='1035500'>activations,</span> <span m='1036460'>but</span> <span m='1036640'>this</span>

  <span m='1037660'>only</span> <span m='1037930'>thing</span> <span m='1038260'>that</span>
  <span m='1038380'>actually</span> <span m='1038829'>happens</span> <span m='1039390'>in</span>
  <span m='1039569'>a neural</span> <span m='1039700'>net.</span> </p><p><span m='1041260'>What</span>
  <span m='1041650'>we</span> <span m='1041770'>also</span> <span m='1042130'>have</span>

  <span m='1045700'>will</span> <span m='1045849'>be</span> <span m='1046000'>talking</span>
  <span m='1046390'>about</span> <span m='1047560'>next.</span> <span m='1048880'>For</span>
  <span m='1049060'>now,</span> <span m='1049930'>we</span> <span m='1050090'>will</span>
  <span m='1050340'>dig</span> <span m='1050650'>deeper</span> <span m='1051140'>into</span>
  <span m='1051340'>the</span> <span m='1051490'>activation,</span> <span m='1052210'>and</span>
  <span m='1052420'>specifically,</span> <span m='1053190'>what</span> <span m='1053410'>activation</span>
  <span m='1054040'>functions</span> <span m='1054460'>to</span> <span m='1054580'>use.</span>
  <span m='1055240'>In</span> <span m='1055360'>that</span> <span m='1055570'>case,</span>
  <span m='1056090'>we</span> <span m='1056110'>can</span> <span m='1056290'>see</span>
  <span m='1056590'>that</span> <span m='1058230'>that's a</span> <span m='1058330'>neuron,</span>
  <span m='1058810'>and</span> <span m='1058930'>what</span> <span m='1059140'>the
  neuron</span> <span m='1059470'>is</span> <span m='1059680'>doing</span> <span m='1060070'>here</span>
  <span m='1060400'>is</span> <span m='1060580'>the</span> <span m='1060700'>weighted</span>
  <span m='1060890'>sum</span> <span m='1061390'>that</span> <span m='1061540'>we</span>
  <span m='1061660'>talked</span> <span m='1061870'>about,</span> <span m='1062290'>or
  the dot</span> <span m='1062590'>product.</span> <span m='1063620'>And</span> <span

  <span m='1064420'>from</span> <span m='1064630'>this</span> <span m='1064860'>would</span>
  <span m='1064990'>be</span> <span m='1066100'>fed</span> <span m='1066400'>into</span>
  <span m='1066730'>a</span> <span m='1066840'>certain</span> <span m='1067150'>activation</span>
  <span m='1067810'>function.</span> <span m='1068480'>Common</span> <span m='1068830'>activation</span>
  <span m='1069400'>functions</span> <span m='1069850'>are</span> <span m='1069970'>sigmoid,</span>
  <span m='1070270'>tanh,</span> <span m='1070960'>or</span> <span m='1071500'>rectify</span>
  <span m='1072050'>linear</span> <span m='1072360'>unit,</span> <span m='1073390'>and</span>
  <span m='1074290'>we</span> <span m='1074410'>will</span> <span m='1074590'>go</span>
  <span m='1074850'>through</span> <span m='1075020'>each</span> <span m='1075280'>one</span>
  <span m='1075490'>independently.</span> </p><p><span m='1076190'>So</span> <span
  m='1076450'>here,</span> <span m='1076740'>we</span> <span m='1076870'>can</span>
  <span m='1077080'>see</span> <span m='1078000'>the</span> <span m='1078250'>sigmoid</span>
  <span m='1078820'>activation</span> <span m='1079360'>function.</span> <span m='1079690'>So</span>
  <span m='1079940'>what</span> <span m='1080050'>this</span> <span m='1080230'>function</span>
  <span m='1080560'>essentially</span> <span m='1081130'>does</span> <span m='1081490'>is</span>
  <span m='1082000'>map</span> <span m='1082480'>any</span> <span m='1082750'>input</span>
  <span m='1083604'>to an</span> <span m='1084031'>output</span> <span m='1084460'>in</span>
  <span m='1084610'>the</span> <span m='1084730'>range</span> <span m='1085210'>of</span>
  <span m='1085480'>zero</span> <span m='1085750'>to</span> <span m='1085970'>one,</span>
  <span m='1086595'>and</span> <span m='1086890'>it's</span> <span m='1087070'>defined</span>
  <span m='1087430'>as</span> <span m='1087640'>one</span> <span m='1087860'>divided</span>
  <span m='1088160'>by</span> <span m='1088360'>one</span> <span m='1088770'>plus</span>
  <span m='1088890'>e</span> <span m='1089110'>to the</span> <span m='1089230'>minus</span>
  <span m='1089535'>x.</span> <span m='1090970'>The</span> <span m='1091180'>other</span>
  <span m='1091480'>common</span> <span m='1091780'>activation</span> <span m='1092330'>function</span>
  <span m='1092650'>is</span> <span m='1092860'>tanh,</span> <span m='1093700'>and</span>
  <span m='1093830'>that's</span> <span m='1094210'>any</span> <span m='1094420'>input</span>
  <span m='1095370'>to</span> <span m='1095460'>an</span> <span m='1095810'>output</span>
  <span m='1096160'>between</span> <span m='1096490'>minus</span> <span m='1096880'>one</span>
  <span m='1097090'>and</span> <span m='1097210'>one.</span> <span m='1098320'>And</span>
  <span m='1098450'>then</span> <span m='1098890'>finally,</span> <span m='1099430'>would</span>
  <span m='1099510'>be the</span> <span m='1099700'>rectified</span> <span m='1100310'>linear</span>
  <span m='1100660'>unit,</span> <span m='1101350'>which</span> <span m='1101890'>maps</span>
  <span m='1102320'>an</span> <span m='1102450'>input</span> <span m='1102820'>to</span>
  <span m='1102970'>itself</span> <span m='1103420'>if</span> <span m='1103600'>it's</span>
  <span m='1103750'>positive,</span> <span m='1104470'>or to</span> <span m='1104710'>zero</span>
  <span m='1105080'>if</span> <span m='1105250'>it's</span> <span m='1105430'>negative.</span>
  </p><p><span m='1107440'>Now,</span> <span m='1107740'>in</span> <span m='1107920'>theory,</span>
  <span m='1108985'>you</span> <span m='1109360'>could</span> <span m='1109540'>use</span>
  <span m='1109810'>any</span> <span m='1110050'>function</span> <span m='1110590'>as</span>
  <span m='1110770'>an</span> <span m='1110920'>activation</span> <span m='1111580'>function</span>
  <span m='1112930'>in</span> <span m='1113080'>your</span> <span m='1113200'>network,</span>
  <span m='1113930'>but</span> <span m='1113950'>that's</span> <span m='1114160'>not</span>
  <span m='1114280'>what</span> <span m='1114460'>you</span> <span m='1114610'>want</span>
  <span m='1114820'>to</span> <span m='1114880'>do</span> <span m='1115030'>in</span>
  <span m='1115150'>practice.</span> <span m='1116290'>You</span> <span m='1116470'>want</span>
  <span m='1116680'>your</span> <span m='1116890'>activation</span> <span m='1117460'>functions</span>
  <span m='1118000'>to</span> <span m='1118150'>be</span> <span m='1118330'>non-linear</span>
  <span m='1119680'>for</span> <span m='1119890'>one</span> <span m='1120380'>main

  </p><p><span m='1137320'>And</span> <span m='1137560'>there's</span> <span m='1137780'>a</span>

  <span m='1466630'>also</span> <span m='1466930'>happens</span> <span m='1468070'>occasionally</span>

  <span m='1489010'>going</span> <span m='1489130'>to</span> <span m='1489190'>be</span>
  <span m='1489310'>relevant</span> <span m='1489730'>to</span> <span m='1489880'>your</span>
  <span m='1490150'>classification.</span> </p><p><span m='1492130'>And</span> <span

  <span m='1495470'>or</span> <span m='1495660'>average</span> <span m='1496040'>pooling.</span>
  <span m='1496825'>We</span> <span m='1497250'>will</span> <span m='1497490'>describe</span>
  <span m='1498740'>max</span> <span m='1498990'>pooling</span> <span m='1499410'>here.</span>
  <span m='1500280'>So</span> <span m='1500430'>what</span> <span m='1500580'>happens</span>
  <span m='1501000'>in</span> <span m='1501100'>max</span> <span m='1501360'>pooling</span>

  <span m='1502610'>are</span> <span m='1502680'>dividing</span> <span m='1503160'>the</span>

  <span m='1510310'>if</span> <span m='1510330'>we</span> <span m='1510420'>consider</span>
  <span m='1511230'>two</span> <span m='1511410'>by</span> <span m='1511590'>two</span>

  <span m='1513250'>split</span> <span m='1513480'>the</span> <span m='1513660'>image,</span>
  <span m='1514020'>which</span> <span m='1514320'>in that</span> <span m='1514660'>case

  <span m='1517370'>and</span> <span m='1517440'>for</span> <span m='1517680'>each</span>
  <span m='1518360'>two</span> <span m='1518540'>by</span> <span m='1518730'>two</span>
  <span m='1518910'>square,</span> <span m='1519450'>we</span> <span m='1519570'>would</span>
  <span m='1519840'>take the</span> <span m='1519960'>maximum.</span> <span m='1521370'>In

  <span m='1523590'>then</span> <span m='1523800'>eight,</span> <span m='1524160'>then</span>
  <span m='1524340'>three,</span> <span m='1524610'>then</span> <span m='1524700'>four.</span>
  </p><p><span m='1525480'>And</span> <span m='1526320'>the</span> <span m='1526410'>reason</span>
  <span m='1526770'>that</span> <span m='1526920'>actually</span> <span m='1527280'>works</span>

  <span m='1529050'>you</span> <span m='1529200'>want</span> <span m='1529440'>to</span>
  <span m='1529590'>do</span> <span m='1529740'>is</span> <span m='1529860'>really</span>
  <span m='1530040'>keep</span> <span m='1530340'>track</span> <span m='1530940'>of</span>
  <span m='1531750'>the</span> <span m='1533130'>response</span> <span m='1533730'>of</span>
  <span m='1533880'>the</span> <span m='1534000'>neurons</span> <span m='1534480'>that--</span>
  <span m='1534930'>or</span> <span m='1535240'>the</span> <span m='1535390'>highest</span>
  <span m='1535740'>response</span> <span m='1536250'>produced</span> <span m='1536670'>by</span>
  <span m='1536850'>your</span> <span m='1537120'>neurons.</span> <span m='1538130'>In
  that</span> <span m='1538410'>case,</span> <span m='1538800'>for</span> <span m='1538950'>example,</span>
  <span m='1539430'>the</span> <span m='1539520'>first</span> <span m='1540030'>highest</span>
  <span m='1540360'>response</span> <span m='1540780'>in</span> <span m='1540870'>the</span>
  <span m='1540960'>first</span> <span m='1541240'>square is</span> <span m='1541490'>six,</span>
  <span m='1542310'>and</span> <span m='1542430'>that</span> <span m='1542730'>means</span>
  <span m='1543150'>that</span> <span m='1543720'>if</span> <span m='1544110'>you</span>
  <span m='1544230'>get</span> <span m='1544530'>that</span> <span m='1544770'>high
  of</span> <span m='1545100'>a</span> <span m='1545190'>response,</span> <span m='1545610'>it

  <span m='1547350'>in the</span> <span m='1547470'>image,</span> <span m='1548020'>or</span>
  <span m='1548140'>has</span> <span m='1548280'>been</span> <span m='1548460'>detected.</span>
  <span m='1549090'>And</span> <span m='1549660'>this</span> <span m='1549850'>is</span>
  <span m='1550110'>something</span> <span m='1550680'>you</span> <span m='1550740'>want</span>
  <span m='1550860'>to</span> <span m='1550920'>keep</span> <span m='1551100'>track</span>
  <span m='1551430'>of</span> <span m='1551580'>as</span> <span m='1551940'>you move</span>
  <span m='1552330'>forward in your</span> <span m='1552540'>network.</span> </p><p><span

  <span m='1563880'>you</span> <span m='1564270'>only</span> <span m='1564570'>care</span>
  <span m='1564780'>about</span> <span m='1565020'>the</span> <span m='1565080'>fact</span>
  <span m='1565470'>that</span> <span m='1565770'>something</span> <span m='1566370'>has</span>
  <span m='1566650'>been</span> <span m='1566830'>detected</span> <span m='1567240'>in</span>
  <span m='1567330'>the</span> <span m='1567420'>image.</span> <span m='1567930'>At</span>

  </p><p><span m='1582070'>So</span> <span m='1582450'>if</span> <span m='1582630'>you</span>

  <span m='1598200'>go</span> <span m='1598380'>from</span> <span m='1598530'>224</span>
  <span m='1599370'>by</span> <span m='1599520'>224</span> <span m='1599950'>by</span>
  <span m='1600120'>64</span> <span m='1601160'>to</span> <span m='1601290'>112</span>

  <span m='1602760'>64,</span> <span m='1603450'>and</span> <span m='1603760'>that</span>
  <span m='1603930'>would</span> <span m='1604080'>be</span> <span m='1604200'>reducing</span>

  </p><p><span m='1629240'>So</span> <span m='1629300'>these</span> <span m='1629540'>are,</span>

  <span m='1635580'>doing</span> <span m='1636100'>is</span> <span m='1636380'>repeating</span>
  <span m='1636635'>these</span> <span m='1636890'>steps</span> <span m='1637300'>on</span>
  <span m='1637450'>a</span> <span m='1637875'>certain</span> <span m='1638370'>number</span>

  <span m='1639490'>your</span> <span m='1639930'>network.</span> <span m='1640380'>But</span>
  <span m='1640590'>eventually,</span> <span m='1641220'>you</span> <span m='1641520'>have</span>
  <span m='1641760'>to</span> <span m='1641850'>make</span> <span m='1642220'>a classification,</span>
  <span m='1643070'>and</span> <span m='1643540'>decide</span> <span m='1644730'>in</span>
  <span m='1644910'>our</span> <span m='1645060'>case,</span> <span m='1645390'>whether</span>
  <span m='1645660'>our</span> <span m='1646080'>image</span> <span m='1646380'>has</span>
  <span m='1646650'>a</span> <span m='1646710'>chair</span> <span m='1647010'>or</span>
  <span m='1647100'>doesn't</span> <span m='1647400'>have</span> <span m='1647640'>a</span>
  <span m='1647690'>chair.</span> <span m='1648450'>So</span> <span m='1648750'>how</span>
  <span m='1648900'>does</span> <span m='1649050'>that</span> <span m='1649260'>happen?</span>
  <span m='1650230'>So</span> <span m='1650400'>after</span> <span m='1650680'>you</span>
  <span m='1650820'>perform</span> <span m='1651300'>all</span> <span m='1651510'>these</span>
  <span m='1651660'>steps,</span> <span m='1653130'>there's</span> <span m='1653360'>a</span>
  <span m='1653430'>step</span> <span m='1653820'>that</span> <span m='1653970'>happens</span>
  <span m='1654390'>here</span> <span m='1655350'>that</span> <span m='1655530'>would</span>
  <span m='1655690'>allow</span> <span m='1655940'>you to</span> <span m='1656130'>make</span>
  <span m='1656350'>that</span> <span m='1656640'>prediction,</span> <span m='1657370'>and</span>
  <span m='1657670'>that</span> <span m='1657890'>step</span> <span m='1658240'>is</span>
  <span m='1658380'>usually</span> <span m='1658780'>called</span> <span m='1659180'>a</span>
  <span m='1659630'>fully</span> <span m='1660130'>connected</span> <span m='1660420'>layer,</span>
  <span m='1660960'>or</span> <span m='1661200'>a</span> <span m='1661400'>multi-layer</span>
  <span m='1661870'>perception.</span> </p><p><span m='1663225'>And</span> <span m='1663630'>what</span>
  <span m='1663870'>this</span> <span m='1664080'>essentially</span> <span m='1664650'>is</span>
  <span m='1665250'>is</span> <span m='1665790'>layers</span> <span m='1666190'>that
  are</span> <span m='1666450'>very</span> <span m='1666690'>similar,</span> <span

  <span m='1667820'>same</span> <span m='1668100'>as</span> <span m='1668220'>what</span>
  <span m='1668400'>you</span> <span m='1668520'>had</span> <span m='1668670'>before,</span>
  <span m='1669120'>except</span> <span m='1669510'>that</span> <span m='1669630'>every</span>
  <span m='1669960'>neuron</span> <span m='1670440'>in the</span> <span m='1670710'>layer</span>
  <span m='1670980'>is</span> <span m='1671160'>connected</span> <span m='1671580'>to</span>
  <span m='1671790'>all</span> <span m='1672090'>the</span> <span m='1672210'>previous</span>
  <span m='1672660'>neurons.</span> <span m='1673690'>So</span> <span m='1673740'>what</span>
  <span m='1673890'>it's allowed</span> <span m='1674220'>you</span> <span m='1674360'>to</span>
  <span m='1674590'>do</span> <span m='1674880'>is</span> <span m='1675090'>really</span>
  <span m='1676290'>consider</span> <span m='1677400'>everything</span> <span m='1677960'>you</span>
  <span m='1678120'>currently</span> <span m='1678610'>have</span> <span m='1678930'>about</span>
  <span m='1679180'>your input,</span> <span m='1679360'>or</span> <span m='1679740'>everything</span>
  <span m='1680170'>that's</span> <span m='1680430'>left about</span> <span m='1680690'>your</span>
  <span m='1681000'>input,</span> <span m='1681880'>and</span> <span m='1682500'>compute</span>
  <span m='1682755'>a dot</span> <span m='1683010'>product</span> <span m='1683630'>on</span>
  <span m='1683800'>that,</span> <span m='1685080'>rather</span> <span m='1685320'>than</span>
  <span m='1685530'>focusing</span> <span m='1686010'>on</span> <span m='1686160'>a</span>

  <span m='1687600'>your</span> <span m='1687720'>input</span> <span m='1689340'>like</span>
  <span m='1689580'>previous</span> <span m='1689880'>layers</span> <span m='1690240'>do.</span>
  </p><p><span m='1691740'>In</span> <span m='1691860'>that</span> <span m='1692070'>case,</span>
  <span m='1692760'>if</span> <span m='1692910'>you're</span> <span m='1693090'>actually</span>
  <span m='1693870'>trying</span> <span m='1694140'>to</span> <span m='1694290'>classify</span>
  <span m='1694900'>your</span> <span m='1695040'>input</span> <span m='1695310'>into</span>
  <span m='1695520'>four</span> <span m='1695820'>classes,</span> <span m='1696620'>you</span>
  <span m='1696950'>would</span> <span m='1697130'>ideally</span> <span m='1697340'>have</span>
  <span m='1697950'>four</span> <span m='1698250'>different</span> <span m='1698580'>neurons</span>
  <span m='1698830'>in</span> <span m='1699140'>your</span> <span m='1699370'>output</span>

  <span m='1701820'>of</span> <span m='1701910'>the</span> <span m='1702030'>classes</span>
  <span m='1702480'>that</span> <span m='1702570'>you</span> <span m='1702750'>have,</span>
  <span m='1704070'>and</span> <span m='1704110'>then</span> <span m='1704940'>you</span>
  <span m='1705120'>would</span> <span m='1705870'>perform</span> <span m='1706290'>the</span>
  <span m='1706380'>same</span> <span m='1706680'>operation</span> <span m='1707220'>as</span>
  <span m='1707460'>you</span> <span m='1707670'>would in</span> <span m='1708010'>a
  previous</span> <span m='1708220'>layer,</span> <span m='1708480'>compute</span>
  <span m='1708810'>the dot</span> <span m='1709140'>product,</span> <span m='1709920'>and</span>
  <span m='1710040'>then</span> <span m='1710340'>once</span> <span m='1710640'>you</span>
  <span m='1710820'>obtain</span> <span m='1712180'>the values</span> <span m='1712460'>at
  every</span> <span m='1712710'>neuron,</span> <span m='1713570'>you would</span>
  <span m='1714000'>perform</span> <span m='1714270'>a</span> <span m='1714540'>normalization</span>
  <span m='1715200'>operation</span> <span m='1715870'>on</span> <span m='1716030'>all
  the</span> <span m='1716150'>output.</span> </p><p><span m='1716940'>This</span>
  <span m='1717210'>organization</span> <span m='1717840'>operation</span> <span m='1718230'>is</span>
  <span m='1718380'>called</span> <span m='1718640'>softmax,</span> <span m='1719430'>or</span>
  <span m='1719600'>normalized</span> <span m='1720130'>exponential,</span> <span

  <span m='1721590'>does</span> <span m='1721920'>is</span> <span m='1722020'>really,</span>
  <span m='1722280'>put</span> <span m='1722610'>more</span> <span m='1722940'>weight</span>
  <span m='1723300'>on</span> <span m='1723450'>the</span> <span m='1723570'>highest</span>
  <span m='1723850'>value.</span> <span m='1724800'>And</span> <span m='1725250'>by</span>
  <span m='1725460'>computing</span> <span m='1726040'>the</span> <span m='1726150'>softmax</span>
  <span m='1726940'>at</span> <span m='1727050'>the</span> <span m='1727200'>output,</span>
  <span m='1727740'>you're</span> <span m='1727950'>able</span> <span m='1728160'>to</span>
  <span m='1728340'>compute</span> <span m='1729040'>the</span> <span m='1729160'>posterior</span>
  <span m='1729810'>probabilities,</span> <span m='1730190'>and</span> <span m='1731190'>allows</span>
  <span m='1731490'>you</span> <span m='1731580'>to</span> <span m='1731790'>make</span>
  <span m='1732060'>a</span> <span m='1732150'>more</span> <span m='1732450'>informed--</span>
  <span m='1732730'>or</span> <span m='1733010'>basically</span> <span m='1733410'>make
  a</span> <span m='1733770'>classification</span> <span m='1734460'>decision</span>
  <span m='1735090'>on</span> <span m='1735180'>your</span> <span m='1735370'>input.</span>
  <span m='1737730'>Great.</span> <span m='1738850'>So</span> <span m='1739680'>that's</span>
  <span m='1739935'>everything.</span> <span m='1741182'>And now,</span> <span m='1741680'>the</span>
  <span m='1741800'>next</span> <span m='1742020'>step</span> <span m='1742300'>will</span>
  <span m='1742400'>be</span> <span m='1742560'>talking</span> <span m='1742955'>about</span>
  <span m='1743350'>back</span> <span m='1743690'>propagation.</span> </p><p><span
  m='1745504'>ISHWARYA ANANTHABHOTLA:</span> <span m='1745740'>OK.</span> <span m='1746450'>So</span>
  <span m='1746620'>now</span> <span m='1746740'>that Henry</span> <span m='1747000'>has</span>
  <span m='1747260'>given</span> <span m='1747400'>us an</span> <span m='1747670'>overview</span>
  <span m='1747940'>of the</span> <span m='1748230'>entire</span> <span m='1748640'>architecture</span>
  <span m='1749040'>of a CNN,</span> <span m='1749620'>I'm</span> <span m='1749940'>going</span>
  <span m='1750050'>to</span> <span m='1750110'>quickly</span> <span m='1750385'>spend
  some</span> <span m='1750660'>time,</span> <span m='1751000'>and</span> <span m='1751350'>talk</span>
  <span m='1751620'>about</span> <span m='1751980'>standard</span> <span m='1752430'>preprocessing</span>
  <span m='1753760'>tricks</span> <span m='1754170'>and tips</span> <span m='1754610'>that</span>
  <span m='1754770'>people</span> <span m='1754980'>might</span> <span m='1755220'>use</span>
  <span m='1755790'>on the</span> <span m='1756030'>image</span> <span m='1756315'>dataset</span>
  <span m='1757020'>before</span> <span m='1757320'>they</span> <span m='1757380'>actually</span>
  <span m='1757740'>feet it</span> <span m='1758160'>through</span> <span m='1759310'>a
  neural</span> <span m='1759600'>net to</span> <span m='1759820'>classify the</span>
  <span m='1760265'>images.</span> <span m='1761600'>So</span> <span m='1762440'>let's</span>
  <span m='1762720'>suppose</span> <span m='1763080'>we</span> <span m='1763200'>have</span>
  <span m='1763290'>a</span> <span m='1763680'>dataset</span> <span m='1764100'>x,</span>
  <span m='1764580'>and</span> <span m='1764880'>there</span> <span m='1765240'>are</span>
  <span m='1765290'>n</span> <span m='1765460'>number</span> <span m='1765670'>of</span>
  <span m='1765960'>data points</span> <span m='1766260'>in the</span> <span m='1766640'>dataset,</span>
  <span m='1766900'>and each</span> <span m='1767386'>point has</span> <span m='1767872'>a</span>
  <span m='1768358'>dimension,</span> <span m='1768844'>D.</span> <span m='1769450'>So</span>
  <span m='1769770'>they</span> <span m='1770090'>have</span> <span m='1770400'>D</span>
  <span m='1770760'>features</span> <span m='1771015'>per</span> <span m='1771270'>point.</span>
  </p><p><span m='1773010'>So</span> <span m='1773340'>in this</span> <span m='1773776'>example,</span>
  <span m='1774212'>we</span> <span m='1774648'>use these</span> <span m='1775084'>graphs
  as an example.</span> <span m='1775520'>Basically,</span> <span m='1775970'>our</span>
  <span m='1776280'>original</span> <span m='1776670'>data</span> <span m='1776960'>here</span>
  <span m='1777250'>has</span> <span m='1777460'>just</span> <span m='1777650'>two
  dimensions,</span> <span m='1778370'>and</span> <span m='1778730'>it</span> <span
  m='1778920'>spans</span> <span m='1779370'>this</span> <span m='1779520'>range</span>
  <span m='1779820'>of</span> <span m='1779880'>values.</span> <span m='1780970'>So</span>
  <span m='1781020'>for</span> <span m='1781120'>example,</span> <span m='1781320'>if
  we</span> <span m='1781780'>want to center</span> <span m='1782110'>this</span>
  <span m='1782463'>data,</span> <span m='1782816'>what we</span> <span m='1783170'>would
  do</span> <span m='1783460'>is a</span> <span m='1783680'>mean</span> <span m='1783980'>subtraction.</span>
  <span m='1784330'>So we</span> <span m='1784680'>basically</span> <span m='1785040'>subtract</span>
  <span m='1785130'>the mean</span> <span m='1785760'>across</span> <span m='1786090'>all</span>
  <span m='1786360'>the</span> <span m='1786600'>features</span> <span m='1787640'>of
  all</span> <span m='1787930'>the points,</span> <span m='1788390'>and we</span>
  <span m='1788620'>basically</span> <span m='1789080'>center it,</span> <span m='1789540'>and</span>
  <span m='1789650'>you</span> <span m='1789730'>can</span> <span m='1789880'>see</span>
  <span m='1790020'>that transformation</span> <span m='1790710'>here.</span> <span
  m='1792120'>And</span> <span m='1792270'>then</span> <span m='1792420'>we</span>
  <span m='1792570'>might,</span> <span m='1792900'>again,</span> <span m='1793230'>go</span>
  <span m='1793440'>for</span> <span m='1793660'>normalizing</span> <span m='1794220'>the</span>
  <span m='1794420'>dimension</span> <span m='1794920'>so that</span> <span m='1795180'>you
  have</span> <span m='1795480'>it.</span> <span m='1795932'>The</span> <span m='1796384'>data
  points</span> <span m='1796836'>span</span> <span m='1797290'>the</span> <span m='1797490'>same</span>
  <span m='1797910'>range</span> <span m='1798270'>of</span> <span m='1798330'>values</span>
  <span m='1798710'>in</span> <span m='1799090'>both</span> <span m='1799190'>dimensions.</span>
  <span m='1800030'>So</span> <span m='1800130'>you</span> <span m='1800190'>can</span>
  <span m='1800310'>see</span> <span m='1800460'>that</span> <span m='1800670'>transformation,</span>
  <span m='1801150'>and</span> <span m='1801630'>how it's taken</span> <span m='1802110'>place
  here.</span> <span m='1802942'>And we</span> <span m='1803360'>just divide</span>
  <span m='1803540'>by the standard</span> <span m='1804007'>deviation</span> <span
  m='1804474'>to do</span> <span m='1804941'>this.</span> </p><p><span m='1807276'>Something</span>
  <span m='1807750'>that's very</span> <span m='1807990'>commonly</span> <span m='1808380'>done
  is</span> <span m='1808710'>called</span> <span m='1808950'>PCA,</span> <span m='1809250'>or</span>
  <span m='1809550'>Principal</span> <span m='1809700'>Component</span> <span m='1810040'>Analysis.</span>
  <span m='1811297'>And</span> <span m='1811704'>the idea</span> <span m='1812111'>here
  is</span> <span m='1812520'>sometimes</span> <span m='1813000'>we have</span> <span
  m='1813090'>a</span> <span m='1813420'>dataset</span> <span m='1813750'>that</span>
  <span m='1813980'>has</span> <span m='1814290'>a</span> <span m='1814350'>very,</span>
  <span m='1814750'>very</span> <span m='1814890'>high</span> <span m='1815080'>dimensionality,</span>
  <span m='1815270'>and</span> <span m='1815740'>we</span> <span m='1816210'>would</span>
  <span m='1816420'>like</span> <span m='1816630'>to</span> <span m='1816960'>reduce</span>
  <span m='1817370'>that</span> <span m='1817540'>dimensionality.</span> <span m='1818910'>So</span>
  <span m='1819150'>basically,</span> <span m='1819540'>what</span> <span m='1819720'>our</span>
  <span m='1819960'>goal</span> <span m='1820350'>is</span> <span m='1820710'>is to</span>
  <span m='1820830'>project</span> <span m='1821260'>the</span> <span m='1821310'>higher</span>
  <span m='1821640'>dimensional</span> <span m='1822300'>space</span> <span m='1823050'>onto</span>
  <span m='1823460'>a lower</span> <span m='1823680'>dimensionality</span> <span m='1824280'>space
  by</span> <span m='1824640'>taking the</span> <span m='1824840'>subset of</span>
  <span m='1825304'>those features.</span> <span m='1827160'>And</span> <span m='1827420'>if</span>
  <span m='1827520'>you've</span> <span m='1827640'>seen</span> <span m='1827910'>a</span>
  <span m='1827940'>little</span> <span m='1828160'>bit of</span> <span m='1828340'>1806</span>
  <span m='1828750'>from</span> <span m='1829010'>linear</span> <span m='1829210'>algebra,</span>
  <span m='1829770'>the</span> <span m='1829880'>way</span> <span m='1830040'>we</span>
  <span m='1830160'>do</span> <span m='1830340'>this</span> <span m='1830580'>is</span>
  <span m='1830730'>by</span> <span m='1830820'>generating</span> <span m='1831600'>a</span>
  <span m='1831780'>covariance</span> <span m='1832230'>matrix,</span> <span m='1832860'>then</span>
  <span m='1833010'>doing</span> <span m='1833180'>the</span> <span m='1833400'>single
  variable</span> <span m='1833540'>decomposition.</span> </p><p><span m='1835070'>And
  I'll</span> <span m='1835550'>gloss</span> <span m='1835680'>over the</span> <span
  m='1835890'>math</span> <span m='1836360'>now,</span> <span m='1836610'>but</span>
  <span m='1837300'>that's</span> <span m='1837630'>the</span> <span m='1837900'>idea.</span>
  <span m='1839310'>And you</span> <span m='1839720'>can see here</span> <span m='1839970'>how
  the</span> <span m='1840230'>original</span> <span m='1840490'>data</span> <span
  m='1840960'>spanned</span> <span m='1841320'>two</span> <span m='1841500'>dimensions.</span>
  <span m='1841980'>I would</span> <span m='1842410'>decorrelate</span> <span m='1842670'>it</span>
  <span m='1842990'>so that</span> <span m='1843170'>it</span> <span m='1843330'>spans
  a</span> <span m='1843605'>single</span> <span m='1843880'>dimension.</span> <span
  m='1844050'>And</span> <span m='1844513'>even</span> <span m='1844976'>with this</span>
  <span m='1845440'>data,</span> <span m='1845590'>you</span> <span m='1846000'>might</span>
  <span m='1846360'>want</span> <span m='1846630'>to</span> <span m='1846720'>ensure</span>
  <span m='1846900'>that</span> <span m='1847130'>it's</span> <span m='1847200'>widened,</span>
  <span m='1847440'>which</span> <span m='1847850'>is</span> <span m='1848190'>the
  same</span> <span m='1848410'>deal.</span> <span m='1848850'>You</span> <span m='1849000'>want</span>
  <span m='1849230'>the</span> <span m='1849510'>values to</span> <span m='1849890'>span</span>
  <span m='1850770'>the</span> <span m='1850890'>same</span> <span m='1851190'>range</span>
  <span m='1851610'>in both</span> <span m='1851996'>dimensions.</span> <span m='1852770'>So</span>
  <span m='1852810'>then</span> <span m='1852960'>you</span> <span m='1853050'>would</span>
  <span m='1854062'>just</span> <span m='1854480'>divide</span> <span m='1854900'>by
  your</span> <span m='1855390'>Eigenvalues to</span> <span m='1855873'>get the</span>
  <span m='1856236'>widened</span> <span m='1856600'>data.</span> </p><p><span m='1859520'>This</span>
  <span m='1859670'>last</span> <span m='1860085'>bit is</span> <span m='1860500'>something</span>
  <span m='1860830'>that's</span> <span m='1861190'>very</span> <span m='1861430'>commonly</span>
  <span m='1861820'>done</span> <span m='1862290'>as a</span> <span m='1862550'>preprocessing</span>
  <span m='1862960'>trick,</span> <span m='1863500'>though</span> <span m='1863710'>people</span>
  <span m='1863940'>aren't</span> <span m='1864250'>entirely</span> <span m='1864790'>sure</span>
  <span m='1865480'>why</span> <span m='1866140'>it</span> <span m='1866320'>works</span>
  <span m='1867670'>very</span> <span m='1868010'>well,</span> <span m='1868980'>or
  that</span> <span m='1869080'>it</span> <span m='1869140'>really does</span> <span
  m='1869350'>help,</span> <span m='1869720'>but it's</span> <span m='1869820'>something</span>
  <span m='1870120'>that</span> <span m='1870250'>people</span> <span m='1870560'>do,</span>
  <span m='1871230'>and it's</span> <span m='1871660'>called</span> <span m='1872090'>data</span>
  <span m='1872250'>augmentation.</span> <span m='1872820'>So</span> <span m='1873170'>basically,</span>
  <span m='1873580'>if I</span> <span m='1873700'>have a</span> <span m='1873970'>dataset</span>
  <span m='1874120'>that</span> <span m='1874582'>contains</span> <span m='1876820'>a

  <span m='1878330'>chairs,</span> <span m='1878600'>a bunch of</span> <span m='1878920'>images

  <span m='1880600'>say,</span> <span m='1880790'>trees,</span> <span m='1881960'>I

  <span m='1883165'>augment</span> <span m='1883510'>that</span> <span m='1883800'>dataset</span>
  <span m='1884440'>further</span> <span m='1885370'>by</span> <span m='1885810'>introducing</span>
  <span m='1886270'>a</span> <span m='1886330'>few</span> <span m='1886510'>variations</span>
  <span m='1887080'>on</span> <span m='1887200'>these</span> <span m='1887520'>same</span>
  <span m='1887980'>images.</span> <span m='1888300'>So</span> <span m='1888610'>I

  <span m='1890510'>reflect</span> <span m='1890750'>it</span> <span m='1891280'>a</span>
  <span m='1891540'>few</span> <span m='1891790'>more,</span> <span m='1892090'>scale,</span>

  <span m='2698630'>that</span> <span m='2698840'>it</span> <span m='2698990'>is</span>
  <span m='2699390'>a</span> <span m='2699540'>guitar,</span> <span m='2700070'>or</span>
  <span m='2700260'>a penguin.</span> <span m='2700620'>So it</span> <span m='2701010'>classifies</span>
  <span m='2701300'>it,</span> <span m='2703190'>and</span> <span m='2703380'>so we</span>
  <span m='2703500'>can</span> <span m='2704160'>use</span> <span m='2706010'>a</span>
  <span m='2706160'>modification</span> <span m='2707340'>of</span> <span m='2708060'>that</span>

  <span m='2709650'>an</span> <span m='2709920'>evolutionary</span> <span m='2710490'>algorithm,</span>

  <span m='2713700'>We</span> <span m='2713790'>take</span> <span m='2714490'>a couple</span>
  <span m='2714890'>of</span> <span m='2715210'>images,</span> <span m='2715620'>and</span>
  <span m='2715740'>we put</span> <span m='2715920'>them</span> <span m='2716040'>through,</span>

  <span m='2718560'>what</span> <span m='2718940'>the</span> <span m='2719090'>classification
